[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Java-based fuzzing run against a PDF text extraction component triggered an [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOutOfMemoryError in the PDFBox font parsing code. The crash, flagged as [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow`, indicates that processing a malformed or specially [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrafted input exhausted the JVM heap during PFB font parsing.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Details  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`com.example.PDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked PDFBox’s text extraction logic on a crafted PDF input. During execution, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe JVM ran out of heap space, leading to a `java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspace`. Jazzer reported this as `FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39muse [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'-Xmx1710m'[0m[39m to reproduce[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is classified by Jazzer as a low-severity fuzzer-detected security [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue due to uncontrolled memory usage. The immediate symptom is a heap exhaustion [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The failure occurs in `org.apache.fontbox.pfb.PfbParser.parsePfb` while [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempting to parse a Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font in PFB format.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace proceeds through `Type1Font.createWithPFB`, [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PDFontFactory.createFont`, and resource handling in `PDResources.getFont`.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Further propagation goes through text-extraction operators in [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SetFontAndSize.process`, and the generic PDF content pipeline in `PDFStreamEngine`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `PDFTextStripper`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness serves only as an entry point; the root issue resides within[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe PDFBox/fontbox components.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.fontbox.pfb.PfbParser` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparticularly `parsePfb` and its buffer [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `org.apache.fontbox.type1.Type1Font.createWithPFB` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandling of parsed PFB [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtracking segment sizes and cumulative total, added bounds checks against a [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAX_LENGTH` limit, and guarded against values exceeding `Integer.MAX_VALUE` before[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocating output buffers. After applying the changes, the build failed with a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation error: “possible lossy conversion from long to int” on an array [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation using a `long`-typed size.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A jazzer-driven fuzz test [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m caused an OOM in FontBox’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PfbParser.parsePfb`.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace shows unbounded reading of “PFB” segments, accumulating in an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`int total` and allocating a byte array of that size.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The OOM arises when a crafted PFB input requests an extremely large segment or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcumulative size.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The parser reads a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte little-endian size into an `int`, then sums segments in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man `int total`.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No check prevents integer overflow or limits how large a byte array may grow, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to excessive memory allocation.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer harness is simply driving the parser with arbitrary data; the root [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause lies in the parser’s unguarded size calculations.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changed `int total` to `long total` for tracking the cumulative byte count.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changed the per-segment size calculation to use a `long size`, masking each byte [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Introduced a check `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || newTotal > MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to throw [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` when limits are exceeded.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After the loop, added a guard against `total > Integer.MAX_VALUE` before [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocating `pfbdata = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m total[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mResulting Build Log  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Compilation failed in `PfbParser.java` at the line allocating a segment buffer: [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m ar = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Error: incompatible types, possible lossy conversion from long to int. The code [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts `new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlong[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which Java rejects without an explicit cast to `int`.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The array allocation points in `PfbParser` where raw buffers are created [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`new [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, `new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m total[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, `cleartomarkSegment`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The definition and value of `MAX_LENGTH`, and whether it fits an `int` or should [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe a `long`.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any other parts of the parser or related classes that assume segment and total [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msizes fit in an `int`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistency of bounds checks and casts before every array allocation in the PFB [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview of the Issue  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The recent patch correctly upgraded the segment `size` and cumulative `total` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables from `int` to `long` and introduced bounds checks against `MAX_LENGTH`. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, Java array allocations require an `int` size; using a `long` directly in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` triggers a “possible lossy conversion from long to int” [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation error. We must therefore explicitly cast the validated `long` values [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mback to `int` when allocating arrays.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Steps to Implement the Fix  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. After reading each segment length into a `long size` and verifying:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - `size >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - `newTotal = total + size` does not exceed `MAX_LENGTH`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     introduce an explicit cast to `int` for the segment buffer allocation.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     For clarity and safety, convert once:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       int intSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m size;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m safe because size ≤ MAX_LENGTH [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m100[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m <[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInteger.MAX_VALUE[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m ar = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mintSize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Update all usages of `new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` to `new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m size[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor via [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`intSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Ensure that the final concatenated buffer allocation uses the same pattern:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtotal > Integer.MAX_VALUE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"PFB data too large: "[0m[39m + total[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m pfbdata = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m total[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Verify that `total` is updated to `newTotal` before any buffer handling. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mThe[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevious patch already added `total = newTotal;`.[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Outline  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `parsePfb` method, locate the segment-allocation block:  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     long size = …; [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     long newTotal = total + size;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || newTotal > MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     total = newTotal;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-    byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m ar = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+    int intSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m size;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+    byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m ar = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mintSize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     int got = [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[39mar[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     … [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mtypeList.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrecordType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mbarrList.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mar[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - At the end of `parsePfb`, ensure the final buffer allocation is likewise cast:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-    pfbdata = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtotal[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtotal > Integer.MAX_VALUE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"PFB data too large: "[0m[39m + total[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+    pfbdata = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m total[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing bounds checks against `MAX_LENGTH` remain intact, preventing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minteger overflow and excessive memory requests.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By casting only after validation, we guarantee that no lossy conversion occurs[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat runtime or compile time.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The data assembly logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreading segments, storing in `barrList`, and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreassembling into `pfbdata`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is unmodified except for the safe casts, so no [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownstream behavior changes.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Casting a `long` to `int` is safe here because `MAX_LENGTH` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m100[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwell below `Integer.MAX_VALUE`. If future maintainers increase `MAX_LENGTH` above [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Integer.MAX_VALUE`, the explicit `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtotal > Integer.MAX_VALUE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or similar check[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor `size` should catch oversize values before the cast.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external dependencies, harness code, or utility classes are modified; thus,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests and fuzz harness remain fully compatible.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References & Consistency  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This pattern mirrors typical Java I/O safety practices: use wider types for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marithmetic to avoid overflow, then cast to `int` only after range-checking.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other parts of PDFBox [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., image parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m use a similar `long`-to-`int` cast[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworkflow when reading large data blocks.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy applying these explicit, checked casts, the compilation errors are resolved, the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal OOM vulnerability is still guarded against, and the parser’s functional [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior is preserved.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
